Actively upgrading the room (the floor was upgraded by one floor, and the room layout and area remained unchanged), which is worthy of recognition, but first said that breakfast could be served on the 24th floor, and then said that the right to use the 24th floor was not enjoyed, which made the active upgrade lose the goodwill brought to the guests. 4. After staying in the hotel for two days, only one employee smiled and greeted the guests when he met them, and the others were expressionless. 5. The shower room only has a nozzle but no overhead shower. After cleaning, the nozzle does not turn to the wall. The Shangri-La brand needs all employees to maintain it together. It is recommended that the hotel leaders go to the Henan Hotel in Zhengzhou - Yuji Hotel VIP Building to learn from it and see how they greatly improve the satisfaction of guests through service.

I don‚Äôt know how to explain it. Is it a franchise store? Or is the breakfast price itself lower than that of other hotels?
Another little incident I would like to remind other guests is that the package I booked includes breakfast for two adults. When my wife and two children (one 11 years old and one 8 years old) were dining, the waiter firmly refused to include one adult breakfast. It was converted into breakfast for two children. In the end, I had no choice but to buy an extra breakfast for children. That is, one adult and two children ‚â§11 years old paid a total of breakfast for two adults and breakfast for one child. When I finally went to the front desk for consultation, the receptionist asked the manager and said that according to their hotel's regulations, breakfast for two adults means two people. The breakfast does not distinguish between adults and children. Regardless of whether it is reasonable or not, the right of interpretation is in the hands of others.
After a while, I received a call from the hotel, saying that they could make a special arrangement and exchange one adult breakfast for two children's breakfast. However, I reported that I had already paid for it and could it be refunded? The answer was no. .
The final suggestion is to be more humane. We do not require the breakfast standard to be the same as that of Sanya Shangri-La (Sanya Shangri-La's standard is that 11 years old and younger have free breakfast). I just hope that like most hotels, one adult breakfast can be replaced with 2 children 11 years old and younger. Breakfast for children aged 10 years old. .
Nothing more, just a suggestion. The possibility of subsequent dealings should theoretically still exist. .

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe River-view King Room

posted:Posted January 26, 2023
msg:It's the first time to write a bad review

The background of the story is like this. I am from Tangxia, Wenzhou. My partner came to Wenzhou from Shanghai and planned to fly to Qingdao with me the next day. This is her first time in Wenzhou.
At the beginning, I felt that Wenzhou did not have many emerging hotels with high cost performance in Shanghai, so I planned to book Shangri-La. I thought this brand was more reliable, and there were suitable river view rooms, so I planned to stay in this hotel for one night. Unfortunately, the flight to Qingdao on the fourth day of the first day was cancelled, and I rebooked the flight on the fifth day of the first day, so I extended another night at this hotel through Ctrip.

A few outrageous experiences in Shangri-La, Wenzhou on the fourth and fifth day of the ***** New Year:
1. I originally booked a deluxe river view room, but when I entered the room, I found that the front desk gave me a parent-child room. The reply from the front desk is: This room type is facing the river, which is better. If you don‚Äôt like the parent-child room, you can remove the things related to children. But logically speaking, no matter how you change the room type, you need to make it clear to the guest when you check in and get the consent of the guest before changing it, right? (Picture 1 is the parent-child room I took, thank you hotel but unfortunately I don‚Äôt have children yet)

2. At 8:30 am on the second day of check-in, I heard the auntie of the house keeping sip Wen Pu: Hello! Serve the sheep! Said that after receiving the check-out information, he was ordered to clean the room. I replied: I said yesterday that there is an extended stay. Unexpectedly, it was not counted this time, and half an hour later at 9:00, someone knocked on the door and said that they were ordered to clean the room. I was very angry because I was completely disturbed, so I called the front desk and asked them what was going on. The answer from the front desk was: a guest said that the room number was wrong. I was thinking, why would I knock on the door twice if I misplaced it? very funny. (I opened DND because of this)

3. I thought about the previous few things that were too big for Chinese New Year, but when I returned to the room after dinner, I found that the card could not be swiped. We used the landline at the entrance of the elevator to tell the front desk that the card could not be used, and the front desk said to come and have a look, but no one came after waiting for 10 minutes. I thought it was because the front desk was very busy during the Chinese New Year, so I went downstairs to find them directly, and found that they were quite free. I was angry and said to call your room manager to come out! The manager didn't come out. The reason they couldn't swipe the card was that I only booked for one night, so the card was invalid, but when I checked in, I made a point of saying that I would stay for another night. Thinking of the previous few incidents, I was very angry. I said the first two incidents at once, saying why Shangri-La is like this. The young lady at the front desk apologized to me and said to give us a fruit plate. A classmate of mine who works in the hotel said that they should upgrade the room type for such outrageous things, but they said the occupancy rate was full, so I accepted the fruit plate.

4. I apologized for the fruit plate above. After returning to the room and waiting for half an hour, the fruit plate did not come. My partner said that these fruits were freshly picked, hahaha! We wanted to go out for supper, so I called the front desk first and asked that it could be delivered to the room when we went out. As a result, we returned to the room at 10:30 and still didn't see the fruit plate? ? ? I called, and it was delivered right away. The fruit plate delivered was very shabby (Picture 2), and it cost less than 10 yuan. It should be the leftovers from breakfast. (üêÇ)

5. The socket is bad, and the plug will fall off, causing the charging to be disconnected halfway.

As a Wenzhou local, I feel that these outrageous things really disgrace Wenzhou and Shangri-La, and I even wondered whether this hotel has bad feng shui, not the reason for hotel management training. I have also worked in the Peninsula Hotel in Shanghai, but not in the housekeeping department. As we all know, the service attitude of the Peninsula Hotel is first-class and rigorous.
I feel that no matter where you are or what industry you are in, since you are working in a well-known brand hotel, or in a hotel in your hometown, you must be rigorous and at least leave a good impression on people.
